New York 10282. Each officer holds office at the pleasure of the Board until the next election of officers or until his or her successor is duly elected and qualifies. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Brendan McGovern.</B>&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;McGovern has served as chief executive officer and president of the Company since June 2016.
Mr.&nbsp;McGovern heads GSAM&#146;s Private Credit Group, is chief executive officer and president of GS BDC, PMMC and PMMC II and also serves <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">as&nbsp;co-head&nbsp;and</FONT> senior portfolio manager of the GSAM
Credit Alternatives portfolio management team. He is also the Chair and a voting member of the Private Credit Group&#146;s Investment Committee, which is responsible for evaluating and approving all of the Company&#146;s investments.
Mr.&nbsp;McGovern joined the firm in 2006. Prior to joining the firm, Mr.&nbsp;McGovern served as a managing director in the Global Investment Group at Amaranth Advisors, where <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">he&nbsp;co-headed&nbsp;the</FONT>
fund&#146;s private placement efforts for both debt and equity linked products in the United States. He is also on the board of directors for the Oxalosis and Hyperoxaluria Foundation. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Jon Yoder.</B>&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;Yoder has served as chief operating officer of the Company since June 2016. Mr.&nbsp;Yoder is the chief
operating officer of GS BDC, PMMC and PMMC II and a member of GSAM&#146;s Private Credit Group with a focus on sourcing, structuring and executing privately negotiated debt financings. He is also a voting member of the Private Credit Group&#146;s
Investment Committee, which is responsible for evaluating and approving all of the Company&#146;s investments. Mr.&nbsp;Yoder joined the firm in 2005. Prior to joining the firm, he was a member of the mergers and acquisitions and private equity
groups at Paul, Weiss, Rifkind, Wharton&nbsp;&amp; Garrison, LLP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Jonathan Lamm.</B> Mr.&nbsp;Lamm has served as chief financial
officer and treasurer of the Company since June 2016. Mr.&nbsp;Lamm is also the chief financial officer and treasurer of GS BDC, PMMC and PMMC II and chief operating officer of the GSAM Credit Alternatives portfolio management team, responsible for
the operations of the business, including business financials, infrastructure support, and IT project management, as well as the continuous improvement of the control environment. Mr.&nbsp;Lamm is secretary and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">a&nbsp;non-voting&nbsp;member</FONT> of the Private Credit Group&#146;s Investment Committee, which is responsible for evaluating and approving all of the Company&#146;s investments. He joined the firm in 2002. Prior
to joining the firm, Mr.&nbsp;Lamm worked in the securities audit practice at Deloitte&nbsp;&amp; Touche, LLP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Julien Yoo.</B>
Ms.&nbsp;Yoo is the chief compliance officer of the Company and has served in such capacity since June 2019. Ms.&nbsp;Yoo is also the chief compliance officer of GS BDC, PMMC, PMMC II, Goldman Sachs Trust, Goldman Sachs Variable Insurance Trust,
Goldman Sachs Trust II, Goldman Sachs MLP Income Opportunities Fund, Goldman Sachs MLP and Energy Renaissance Fund, and Goldman Sachs ETF Trust. Ms.&nbsp;Yoo joined Goldman Sachs in 2013.&nbsp;Prior to joining Goldman Sachs, Ms.&nbsp;Yoo was a Vice
President in the legal department of Morgan Stanley Investment Management. Prior to joining Morgan Stanley, she was an associate at Shearman&nbsp;&amp; Sterling, LLP and at Swidler Berlin Shereff Friedman, LLP. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">12 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>David Yu.</B> Mr.&nbsp;Yu has served as an executive vice president and Head of Research of
the Company since June 2016. Mr.&nbsp;Yu is executive vice president of GS BDC, PMMC and PMMC II and a member of the GSAM Private Credit Group with a focus on sourcing, structuring and executing privately negotiated debt financings and serves as its
Head of Research. Mr.&nbsp;Yu is a voting member of the Private Credit Group&#146;s Investment Committee, which is responsible for evaluating and approving all of the Company&#146;s investments. Mr.&nbsp;Yu joined the firm in 2006. Prior to joining
the firm, Mr.&nbsp;Yu was an associate in the Global Investments Group at Amaranth Advisors, where he similarly worked with public and private issuers to structure and execute debt and equity financings. Prior to joining Amaranth, he worked in the
Leveraged Finance and Sponsor Coverage Group at CIBC World Markets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Jordan Walter.</B>&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;Walter has served as an executive
vice president of the Company since March 2018. Mr.&nbsp;Walter is executive vice president of GS BDC, PMMC and PMMC II and a member of the GSAM Private Credit Group with a focus on sourcing, structuring and executing privately negotiated debt
financings. He is also a voting member of the Private Credit Group&#146;s Investment Committee, which is responsible for evaluating and approving all of the Company&#146;s investments. Mr.&nbsp;Walter joined the firm in 2014. Prior to joining the
firm, Mr.&nbsp;Walter was a vice president at MCG Capital where he originated and managed middle market debt and equity investments. Prior to joining MCG Capital, Mr.&nbsp;Walter was in the Financial Management Program at General Electric </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Michael Mastropaolo.</B>&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;Mastropaolo has served as an executive vice president of the Company since January 2019.
Mr.&nbsp;Mastropaolo is also an executive vice president of GS BDC and PMMC and a member of the GSAM Credit Alternatives Team with a focus on sourcing, structuring and executing privately negotiated debt financings. He is also a voting member of the
Private Credit Group&#146;s Investment Committee, which is responsible for evaluating and approving all of the Company&#146;s investments. Mr.&nbsp;Mastropaolo joined the firm in 2016. Prior to joining the firm, Mr.&nbsp;Mastropaolo was a Director
at Golub Capital where he originated and managed middle market debt and equity investments. Mr.&nbsp;Mastropaolo began his career investing in middle market credit at General Electric in the Investment Analyst training program at GE Capital. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Carmine Rossetti.</B>&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;Rossetti has served as principal accounting officer of the Company since May 2017. Mr.&nbsp;Rossetti is
also the principal accounting officer of GS BDC, PMMC and PMMC II and head of the GSAM Hedge Fund and BDC Controllers teams. Mr.&nbsp;Rossetti is responsible for fund accounting and financial reporting oversight as well as the continuous improvement
of the control environment. Mr.&nbsp;Rossetti joined Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC in 2004. Prior to joining Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC, he worked in the audit practice at Ernst&nbsp;&amp; Young LLP. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Certain Relationships and Related Party Transactions </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Investment Management and Advisory Agreement </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company is party to an investment management agreement (the &#147;Investment Management Agreement&#148;), pursuant to which the Company
pays GSAM, a wholly owned subsidiary of Group Inc., a quarterly fee for investment management services equal to 0.375% (i.e., an annual rate of 1.50%) of our average NAV (including uninvested cash and cash equivalents), and a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-part</FONT> incentive fee based on (a)&nbsp;the amount by which our ordinary income exceeds certain &#147;hurdle rates,&#148; and (b)&nbsp;our capital gains. Certain of the Company&#146;s officers are also officers and
employees of GSAM. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2018, the Company paid GSAM a total of $7.80&nbsp;million in fees (excluding fees
that are accrued but not paid) pursuant to the Investment Management Agreement, which consisted of $7.80&nbsp;million in management fees and $0.00 in incentive fees. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">13 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>License Agreement </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company is party to a license agreement with an affiliate of Goldman Sachs pursuant to which the Company has been granted <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">a&nbsp;non-exclusive,&nbsp;royalty-free</FONT> license to use the &#147;Goldman Sachs&#148; name. Under this agreement, the Company shall not have a right to use the Goldman Sachs name if GSAM or another affiliate of
Goldman Sachs is not the Company&#146;s Investment Adviser or if the Company&#146;s continued use of such license results in a violation of applicable law, results in a regulatory burden or has adverse regulatory consequences. Other than with
respect to this limited license, the Company has no legal right to the &#147;Goldman Sachs&#148; name. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Investment</FONT> Opportunities </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company has in the past <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-invested,</FONT> and in the future may
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-invest,</FONT> on a concurrent basis with other funds managed by GSAM and its affiliates, but not if such <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-investment</FONT> is impermissible under existing regulatory guidance,
applicable regulations or GSAM&#146;s allocation procedures. Certain types of negotiated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-investments</FONT> may be made only if the Company receives an order from the SEC permitting the Company to do so. On
January&nbsp;4, 2017, the SEC granted the Company, PMMC and GS BDC, as well as certain other funds managed by GSAM in the future, the exemptive relief to make negotiated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-investments,</FONT> subject to certain
terms and conditions in the exemptive relief. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Transfer Agent Agreement </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company has entered into a transfer agency agreement (the &#147;Transfer Agency Agreement&#148;), with Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC, an
affiliate of GSAM, pursuant to which Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC, serves as the Company&#146;s transfer agent (&#147;Transfer Agent&#148;), registrar and disbursing agent. The Company pays the Transfer Agent fees at an annual rate of 0.12% of
the average NAV of the Company at the end of the then-current quarter and the prior calendar quarter (and, in the case of the Company&#146;s first quarter, the Company&#146;s NAV as of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">such&nbsp;quarter-end).</FONT>
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2018, the Company paid Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC a total of $0.62&nbsp;million in fees
pursuant to the Transfer Agent Agreement.<B><I> </I></B> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Placement Agent Agreements </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company has entered into an agreement with each of Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC and Goldman Sachs International (each, a
&#147;Placement Agent&#148; and together with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">various&nbsp;sub-placement&nbsp;agents,</FONT> the &#147;Placement Agents&#148;) pursuant to which the Placement Agents will assist the Company in conducting private
placement offerings. The Placement Agents have entered into or will enter <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">into&nbsp;sub-placement&nbsp;agreements</FONT> (together with the agreements with Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC and Goldman Sachs
International, the &#147;Placement Agent Agreements&#148;) with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">various&nbsp;sub-placement&nbsp;agents</FONT> to assist in conducting the private placement offering. The Placement Agents are not expected to be
compensated by the Company for their services, but may charge investors a placement fee with respect to their investment in the Company. The Placement Agents may also be compensated by the Investment Adviser, in its discretion, for certain services
including promotional and marketing support, shareholder servicing, operational and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">recordkeeping,&nbsp;sub-accounting,&nbsp;networking</FONT> or administrative services. These payments are made out of the Investment
Adviser&#146;s own resources and/or assets, including from the revenues or profits derived from the advisory fees the Investment Adviser receives from the Company. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Related Party Transaction Review Policy </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit Committee conducts quarterly reviews of any potential related party transactions brought to its attention and, during these reviews,
it also considers any conflicts of interest brought to its attention pursuant to the Company&#146;s Code of Ethics. Each of the Company&#146;s directors and executive officers is instructed and </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">14 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
periodically reminded to inform GSAM Compliance of any potential related party transactions. In addition, each such director and executive officer completes a questionnaire on an annual basis
designed to elicit information about any potential related party transactions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Proxy Voting by the Investment Adviser </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our Investment Adviser has implemented processes designed to prevent conflicts of interest from influencing proxy voting decisions that it
makes on behalf of advisory clients, including us, and to help ensure that such decisions are made in accordance with its fiduciary obligations to its clients. Notwithstanding such proxy voting processes, proxy voting decisions made by our
Investment Adviser with respect to securities held by us may benefit the interests of Goldman Sachs and Accounts other than us. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">15 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>PROPOSAL 2 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>RATIFICATION OF SELECTION OF INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At a meeting of the Board held on August <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">7-8,</FONT> 2019, the Audit Committee selected and recommended, and
the Board, including a majority of the Independent Directors, approved, the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to act as the independent registered public accounting firm for the Company for the fiscal year ending December&nbsp;31, 2019. This
selection is presented for ratification by the Stockholders. If the Stockholders fail to ratify the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to serve as the independent registered public accounting firm for the year ending December&nbsp;31, 2019, the
Audit Committee and the Board will reconsider the continued retention of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Representatives of
PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP are expected to be present at the Meeting and will be available to respond to appropriate questions from Stockholders if necessary. Representatives of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP will be given the opportunity to make
statements at the Meeting, if they so desire. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Audit Fees </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The aggregate audit fees billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2018 and for the period from
January&nbsp;11, 2017 (commencement of operations) to December&nbsp;31, 2017 were $300,000 and $250,000, respectively. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fees included in
the audit fees category are those associated with the annual audits of financial statements, review of the financial statements included in the Company&#146;s Quarterly Reports on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Form&nbsp;10-Q&nbsp;and</FONT>
services that are normally provided in connection with statutory and regulatory filings. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Audit-Related Fees </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No audit-related fees were billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2018 and for the period from
January&nbsp;11, 2017 (commencement of operations) to December&nbsp;31, 2017. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Audit-related fees are for any services rendered to the
Company that are reasonably related to the performance of the audits or reviews of the Company&#146;s consolidated financial statements (but not reported as audit fees above). These services include attestation services that are not required by
statute or regulation and consultations concerning financial accounting and reporting standards. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The aggregate audit-related fees billed
by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to GSAM, and any entity controlling, controlled by, or under common control with, GSAM, that provides ongoing services to the Company, for engagements directly related to the Company&#146;s operations and financial
reporting, for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2018 and December&nbsp;31, 2017 were $1,133,433 and $1,133,433, respectively. These amounts represent fees PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP billed to GSAM for services related to SSAE 18 reports. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Tax Fees </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The aggregate fees
billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for services rendered to the Company for tax compliance, tax advice and tax planning for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2018 and for the period from January&nbsp;11, 2017 (commencement of operations) to
December&nbsp;31, 2017 were $58,000 and $10,000, respectively. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fees included in the tax fees category comprise all services performed by
professional staff in the independent registered public accountant&#146;s tax division except those services related to the audits. This category comprises fees for tax compliance services provided in connection with the preparation and review of
the Company&#146;s tax returns. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">16 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No tax fees were billed by the Company&#146;s independent registered public accountant to GSAM,
and any entity controlling, controlled by, or under common control with, GSAM, that provides ongoing services to the Company, for engagements directly related to the Company&#146;s operations and financial reporting, for the years ended
December&nbsp;31, 2018 December&nbsp;31, 2017. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>All Other Fees </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No fees were billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for products and services provided to the Company, other than the services reported in
&#147;Audit Fees,&#148; and &#147;Tax Fees&#148; above, for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2018 and for the period from January&nbsp;11, 2017 (commencement of operations) to December&nbsp;31, 2017. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Other than services reported under &#147;Audit-Related Fees,&#148; no other fees were billed by the Company&#146;s independent registered
public accountant to GSAM, and any entity controlling, controlled by, or under common control with, GSAM, that provides ongoing services to the Company, for engagements directly related to the Company&#146;s operations and financial reporting, for
the for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2018 and for the period from January&nbsp;11, 2017 (commencement of operations) to December&nbsp;31, 2017. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Aggregate <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Audit</FONT> Fees </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">No&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;fees</FONT> were billed to the Company&#146;s investment adviser and service affiliates
by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">for&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services</FONT> for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2018 and for the period from January&nbsp;11, 2017 (commencement of operations) to December&nbsp;31, 2017.
This includes <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">any&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services</FONT> required to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">be&nbsp;pre-approved&nbsp;or&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services</FONT></FONT> that did not
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">require&nbsp;pre-approval&nbsp;since</FONT> they did not directly relate to the Company&#146;s operations or financial reporting. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Pre-Approval</FONT> of Audit and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Audit</FONT> Services Provided to the Company
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">and&nbsp;Non-Audit&nbsp;Services&nbsp;Pre-Approval&nbsp;Policy</FONT></FONT> (the &#147;Policy&#148;) adopted by the Audit Committee sets forth the procedures and the conditions
pursuant to which services performed by an independent auditor for the Company may <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">be&nbsp;pre-approved.&nbsp;Services</FONT> may <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">be&nbsp;pre-approved&nbsp;specifically</FONT> by the
Audit Committee as a whole or, in certain circumstances, by the Audit Committee Chairman or the person designated as the audit committee financial expert. In addition, subject to specified cost limitations, certain services may <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">be&nbsp;pre-approved&nbsp;under</FONT> the provisions of the Policy. The Policy provides that the Audit Committee will consider whether the services provided by an independent auditor are consistent with the SEC&#146;s
rules on auditor independence. The Policy provides for periodic review <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">and&nbsp;pre-approval&nbsp;by</FONT> the Audit Committee of the services that may be provided by the independent auditor. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>De Minimis Waiver</I>. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">The&nbsp;pre-approval&nbsp;requirements</FONT> of the Policy may be waived with
respect to the provision <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services</FONT> that are permissible for an independent auditor to perform, provided (1)&nbsp;the aggregate amount of all such services provided constitutes no more
than five percent of the total amount of revenues subject <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">to&nbsp;pre-approval&nbsp;that</FONT> was paid to the independent auditors during the fiscal year in which the services are provided; (2)&nbsp;such services
were not recognized by the Company at the time of the engagement to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">be&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services;</FONT> and (3)&nbsp;such services are promptly brought to the attention of the Audit Committee and approved prior
to the completion of the audit by the Audit Committee or by one or more members of the Audit Committee to whom authority to grant such approvals has been delegated by the Audit Committee, pursuant to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;pre-approval&nbsp;provisions</FONT> of the Policy. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Pre-Approval</FONT></I><I></I><I>&nbsp;of</I><I></I><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&nbsp;
Non-Audit</FONT></I><I></I><I>&nbsp;Services Provided to GSAM.</I>&nbsp;The Policy provides that, in addition to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">requiring&nbsp;pre-approval&nbsp;of</FONT> audit
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">and&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services</FONT> provided to the Company, the Audit Committee
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">will&nbsp;pre-approve&nbsp;those&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services</FONT></FONT> provided to the Company&#146;s investment adviser (and entities controlling, controlled by or under common
control with the investment adviser that provide ongoing services to the Company) where the engagement relates directly to the operations or financial reporting of the Company. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">17 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit Committee has considered these fees and the nature of the services rendered, and has
concluded that they are compatible with maintaining the independence of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP. The Audit Committee did not approve any of the audit-related, tax, or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">other&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;fees</FONT>
described above pursuant to the &#147;<I>de minimis</I>&nbsp;exceptions&#148; set forth in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Rule&nbsp;2-01(c)(7)(i)(C)&nbsp;and</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Rule&nbsp;2-01(c)(7)(ii)&nbsp;of</FONT> <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Regulation&nbsp;S-X.&nbsp;PricewaterhouseCoopers</FONT> LLP did not provide any audit-related services, tax services or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">other&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services</FONT> to GSAM or any entity
controlling, controlled by or under common control with GSAM that provides ongoing services to the Company that the Audit Committee was required to approve pursuant to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Rule&nbsp;2-01(c)(7)(ii)&nbsp;of</FONT> <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Regulation&nbsp;S-X.&nbsp;The</FONT> Audit Committee considered whether the provision <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-audit&nbsp;services</FONT> rendered to GSAM and any entity controlling, controlled by, or
under common control with GSAM that provides ongoing services to the Company that were <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">not&nbsp;pre-approved&nbsp;by</FONT> the Audit Committee because the engagement did not relate directly to the operations and
financial reporting of the Company is compatible with maintaining PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP&#146;s independence. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>THE BOARD, INCLUDING
EACH OF THE INDEPENDENT DIRECTORS, UNANIMOUSLY RECOMMENDS THAT YOU VOTE&nbsp;&#147;FOR&#148;&nbsp;THE RATIFICATION OF PRICEWATERHOUSECOOPERS LLP AS INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM TO THE COMPANY FOR THE FISCAL YEAR ENDING
DECEMBER&nbsp;31, 2019. </B></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">18 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B></B><B><I>Audit Committee
Report</I></B><B><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&nbsp;(1)</SUP> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following is the report of the Audit Committee of
Goldman Sachs Middle Market Lending Corp. (the &#147;Company&#148;) with respect to the Company&#146;s audited financial statements as of December&nbsp;31, 2018 (the &#147;Audited Financial Statements&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit Committee has: (a)&nbsp;reviewed and discussed the Audited Financial Statements with the management of the Company;
(b)&nbsp;discussed with the independent auditor the matters required to be discussed by the Public Company Accounting Oversight Board (&#147;PCAOB&#148;) Standard No.&nbsp;1301, as modified or supplemented; and (c)&nbsp;received the written
disclosures and the letter from the independent auditor required by applicable requirements of the PCAOB Ethics and Independence Rule 3526 regarding the independent auditor&#146;s communications with the Audit Committee concerning independence, and
has discussed with the independent auditor the auditor&#146;s independence. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The members of the Audit Committee are not, and do not
represent themselves to be, professionally engaged in the practice of auditing or accounting and are not employed by the Company for accounting, financial management or internal control purposes. Moreover, the Audit Committee relies on and makes no
independent verification of the facts presented to it or representations made by management or the Company&#146;s independent auditor. Accordingly, the Audit Committee&#146;s oversight does not provide an independent basis to determine that
management has maintained appropriate accounting and/or financial reporting principles and policies, or internal controls and procedures designed to assure compliance with accounting standards and applicable laws and regulations. Furthermore, the
Audit Committee&#146;s considerations and discussions referred to above do not provide assurance that the audit of the Company&#146;s financial statements has been carried out in accordance with the standards of the PCAOB or that the financial
statements are presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Based on its consideration of the Audited Financial
Statements and the discussions referred to above with management and the Company&#146;s independent auditor, and subject to the limitations on the responsibilities and role of the Audit Committee set forth in the charter and those discussed above,
the Audit Committee recommended to the Board of Directors that the Audited Financial Statements be accepted by the Board of Directors and included in the Company&#146;s Annual Report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K</FONT> for the last
fiscal year for filing with the SEC. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">August&nbsp;7, 2019 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>The Audit Committee </B></P>

</P> <P STYLE="font-size:100pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:11%">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The material in this report is not &#147;soliciting material,&#148; is not deemed &#147;filed&#148; with the

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">19 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>OTHER BUSINESS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The management of the Company does not know of any other matters to be brought before the Meeting. If such matters are properly brought before
the Meeting, proxies that do not contain specific instructions to the contrary will be voted in accordance with the judgment of Caroline Kraus and Joseph McClain, who are the persons named as proxies. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>VOTE REQUIRED FOR THE ELECTION OF DIRECTORS AND APPROVAL OF </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>OTHER MATTERS AT THE MEETING </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A quorum for the transaction of business at the Meeting is established by the presence, in person or by proxy, of holders representing a
majority of the votes entitled to be cast at the Meeting. Stockholders of record at the close of business on the Record Date are entitled to receive notice of, and to vote at, the Meeting and at any postponements or adjournments thereof.&nbsp;There
were 49,470,257&nbsp;shares of the Company&#146;s common stock outstanding on the Record Date. Each share of common stock is entitled to one vote. Cumulative voting is not permitted. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Election of Directors </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The election of
each nominee requires a majority of the votes cast by all Stockholders present, in person or by proxy, at the Meeting, provided that if, as of the tenth (10th)&nbsp;day preceding the date the Company first mails the notice of such meeting to the
Stockholders, the number of nominees for the directorships (or, if applicable, the directorships of a particular class of directors) exceeds the number of such directors to be elected, such directors shall be elected by the vote of a plurality of
the votes cast. Under the Company&#146;s bylaws, a majority of votes cast means that the number of votes cast &#147;for&#148; a director&#146;s election exceeds the number of votes cast &#147;against&#148; that director&#146;s election (with
&#147;abstentions&#148; and &#147;broker <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-votes&#148;</FONT> not counted as a vote cast either &#147;for&#148; or &#147;against&#148; that director&#146;s election). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Ratification of Auditor </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Approval of
Proposal 2, the ratification of the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to serve as the Company&#146;s independent registered public accounting firm, requires a majority of the votes cast by all Stockholders present, in person or by proxy, at
the Meeting. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Broker <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Votes</FONT> </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Broker <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;non-votes&#148;</FONT> are shares held in an account with an Authorized Institution for which the
broker indicates that instructions have not been received from the beneficial owners or other persons entitled to vote, and the broker does not have discretionary voting authority with respect to a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-routine</FONT>
proposal. As broker <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-votes</FONT> are entitled to vote on Proposal 2, broker <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-votes</FONT> will be counted as shares present for purposes of determining whether a quorum is
present. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Proposal 1 is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-routine</FONT> matter. As a result, if you hold shares in &#147;street
name&#148; through a broker, bank or other nominee, your broker, bank or nominee will<B></B><B>&nbsp;not</B>&nbsp;be permitted to exercise voting discretion with respect to Proposal 1, the election of four directors. Therefore, if you do not vote
and you do not give your broker or other nominee specific instructions on how to vote for you, then your shares will have no effect on Proposal 1. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Proposal 2, the ratification of the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to serve as the Company&#146;s independent registered public
accounting firm, is a routine matter. As a result, if you beneficially own your shares and you do not provide your broker or nominee with voting instructions, then your broker, bank or nominee will be able to vote your shares for you on Proposal 2.
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">20 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Abstentions </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Abstentions will be counted as shares present for purposes of determining whether a quorum is present, but will not be voted for or against the
Proposal for which the proxy card has been marked &#147;Abstain&#148;. Accordingly, abstentions will have no effect on either Proposal. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Adjournment
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If less than a quorum is present at the Meeting or if an insufficient number of votes is present for the approval of the Proposals,
the chairman of the Meeting shall have the power to adjourn the Meeting from time to time without notice other than announcement at the Meeting. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A vote may be taken on either Proposal prior to any such adjournment if there are sufficient votes for approval of such Proposal. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>COMMUNICATIONS WITH THE BOARD </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">All interested parties, including Stockholders, may send communications to the Board, the Independent Directors, the Chairperson or any other
individual director, by addressing such communication to the Board, the Independent Directors, the Chairperson or to the individual director, c/o Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P., 200 West Street, New York, New York 10282. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ANNUAL AND QUARTERLY REPORTS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Copies of the Company&#146;s Annual Reports on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K,</FONT> Quarterly Reports on Form <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-Q</FONT> and Current Reports on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">8-K</FONT> are available, without charge, or upon request by writing to the Company or by calling the Company at (312)
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">655-4702.</FONT> Please direct your written request to Caroline L. Kraus, Secretary, at the Company, c/o Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P., 200 West Street, New York, New York 10282. Copies of such reports are
also posted and are available without charge on the SEC&#146;s website at www.sec.gov. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>CORPORATE GOVERNANCE </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Code of Ethics </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We have adopted a Code of
Ethics pursuant to Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">17j-1</FONT> under the 1940 Act and we have also approved the Company&#146;s Investment Adviser&#146;s Code of Ethics that it adopted in accordance with Rule
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">17j-1</FONT> and Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">204A-1</FONT> under the Investment Advisers Act of 1940, as amended. These Codes of Ethics establish, among other things, procedures for personal investments and
restrict certain personal securities transactions, including transactions in securities that are held by the Company. Personnel subject to each code may invest in securities for their personal investment accounts, so long as such investments are
made in accordance with the code&#146;s requirements. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Code of Business Conduct and Ethics </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We have adopted a Code of Business Conduct and Ethics which applies to, among others, the Company&#146;s Chief Executive Officer and Chief
Financial Officer. The Company intends to disclose any material amendment to or waivers of required provisions of the Code of Business Conduct and Ethics on a current report on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Form&nbsp;8-K.</FONT> </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">21 </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Corporate Governance Guidelines and Director Charter </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We have adopted Corporate Governance Guidelines and a Director Charter which applies to, among other things, the authority and duties of the
directors, the composition of the Board and the election and role of the Chairperson of the Board. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ADDITIONAL INFORMATION </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The principal address of the Company&#146;s Investment Adviser is Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P., 200&nbsp;West Street, New York, New
York 10282. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The principal address of the Company&#146;s administrator is State Street Bank and Trust Company, One Lincoln Street, Boston,
Massachusetts 02111. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>STOCKHOLDER PROPOSALS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company expects that the 2020 Annual Meeting of Stockholders will be held in November 2020, but the exact date, time and location of such
meeting have yet to be determined. A Stockholder who intends to present a proposal at that annual meeting, including nomination of a director, must submit the proposal in writing to the Secretary of the Company, Caroline L. Kraus, c/o Goldman Sachs
Asset Management, L.P., 200 West Street, New&nbsp;York, New York 10282. Notices of intention to present proposals, including nomination of a director, at the 2020 annual meeting must be received by the Company no earlier than July&nbsp;11, 2020 and
no later than 5:00&nbsp;p.m., Eastern Time, on August&nbsp;10, 2020. In order for a proposal to be considered for inclusion in the Company&#146;s proxy statement for the 2020 Annual Meeting, the Company must receive the proposal no later than
May&nbsp;14, 2020. The submission of a proposal does not guarantee its inclusion in the Company&#146;s proxy statement or presentation at the meeting unless certain securities law requirements are met. The Company reserves the right to reject, rule
out of order or take other appropriate action with respect to any proposal that does not comply with these and other applicable requirements. </P>
